[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA Jazzer‐driven fuzzing session against the Apache Commons Compress Expander [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexample uncovered a low-severity security issue: the library throws an [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mOutOfMemoryError when processing certain compressed inputs. The failure is [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclassified as a `FuzzerSecurityIssueLow` due to uncontrolled heap allocation in the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mLZW decompression routine, resulting in a denial-of-service scenario.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue overview  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  While running the ExpanderFuzzer with a custom test case, the Java code in [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Expander.expand` invoked Apache Commons Compress’s LZW decompression path [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`LZWInputStream.initializeTables`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. An unexpectedly large allocation request [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcaused a `java.lang.OutOfMemoryError: Java heap space`. Jazzer reported this as a [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`FuzzerSecurityIssueLow: Out of memory [0m[1;39m([0m[39muse [0m[32m'-Xmx1710m'[0m[39m to reproduce[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  Denial of Service via uncontrolled memory consumption during decompression.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The crash occurs deep in the LZW algorithm’s table initialization [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m186[0m[39m [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand [0m[1;36m220[0m[39m of LZWInputStream[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The call stack shows the failure is triggered by `ZCompressorInputStream` → [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`CompressorStreamFactory.createCompressorInputStream` → `Expander.decompress` → [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Expander.expand` → the fuzzer harness `fuzzerTestOneInput`.  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Jazzer instrumentation and hooks show comprehensive coverage of compression and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdecompression classes, but the input path to LZW remains unchecked.  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The reproducer and libFuzzer crash input were generated, indicating [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeterministic reproduction.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Affected code areas for investigation  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. `org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander` — particularly the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`decompress` and `expand` methods that dispatch to the compressor factory.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. `org.apache.commons.compress.compressors.CompressorStreamFactory` — its logic [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor selecting and instantiating input streams.  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. `org.apache.commons.compress.compressors.z.ZCompressorInputStream` and [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`org.apache.commons.compress.compressors.lzw.LZWInputStream` — focusing on buffer [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msizes, table initialization, and bounds checks.  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Any upstream validation layers or wrappers that might constrain or validate [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muser-provided compressed payload sizes before delegating to the LZW implementation.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNo root-cause speculation or remediation steps are provided here. This report [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdocuments the uncontrolled memory consumption scenario discovered by fuzzing.[0m       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m434[0m[39m:     * Constructs an instance with the decompress Concatenated option set to [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfalse.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m435[0m[39m:     *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m436[0m[39m:    public [0m[1;35mCompressorStreamFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m437[0m[39m:        this.decompressUntilEof = null;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m438[0m[39m:        this.memoryLimitInKb = [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/compressors/z/ZCompressorInputStream.jav[0m[1;92ma[0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m73[0m[39m:    public [0m[1;35mZCompressorInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal InputStream inputStream, final int [0m      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/compressors/z/ZCompressorInputStream.jav[0m[1;92ma[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m:60[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m90[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m60[0m[39m:     * @throws IOException if an I/O error occurs.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m61[0m[39m:     *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m62[0m[39m:    public [0m[1;35mZCompressorInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal InputStream inputStream[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIOException [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m63[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mthis[0m[1;39m([0m[39minputStream, [0m[1;36m-1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m64[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m65[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m66[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[39m**[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m67[0m[39m:     * Constructs a new instance.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m68[0m[39m:     *[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m69[0m[39m:     * @param inputStream The underlying input stream.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m70[0m[39m:     * @param memoryLimitInKiB maximum allowed estimated memory usage in [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mkibibytes.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m71[0m[39m:     * @throws IOException if an I/O error occurs.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m72[0m[39m:     *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m73[0m[39m:    public [0m[1;35mZCompressorInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal InputStream inputStream, final int [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemoryLimitInKiB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException [0m[1;39m{[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m74[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35msuper[0m[1;39m([0m[39minputStream, ByteOrder.LITTLE_ENDIAN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m75[0m[39m:        final int firstByte = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35min.readBits[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m76[0m[39m:        final int secondByte = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35min.readBits[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m77[0m[39m:        final int thirdByte = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35min.readBits[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m78[0m[39m:        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfirstByte != MAGIC_1 || secondByte != MAGIC_2 || thirdByte < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m79[0m[39m:            throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Input is not in .Z format"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m80[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m81[0m[39m:        blockMode = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthirdByte & BLOCK_MODE_MASK[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m82[0m[39m:        maxCodeSize = thirdByte & MAX_CODE_SIZE_MASK;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m83[0m[39m:        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mblockMode[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m84[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35msetClearCode[0m[1;39m([0m[39mDEFAULT_CODE_SIZE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m85[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m86[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCodeSize, memoryLimitInKiB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m87[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mclearEntries[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m88[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m89[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m90[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[39m**[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview and Root Cause  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The uncontrolled heap allocation stems from `ZCompressorInputStream` always [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpassing a negative memory limit [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m into [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mLZWInputStream.initializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCodeSize, memoryLimitInKiB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. Because [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint, int[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` only enforces a limit when `memoryLimitInKiB > [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m`, a [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalue of `[0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m` effectively disables any bound checks, allowing malicious inputs to [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrequest arbitrarily large tables and trigger `OutOfMemoryError`.  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Core Components to Patch  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Class:** `org.apache.commons.compress.compressors.z.ZCompressorInputStream` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Constructors to Modify:**  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • `public [0m[1;35mZCompressorInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream inputStream[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • `public [0m[1;35mZCompressorInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream inputStream, int [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemoryLimitInKiB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Preserve Existing Behavior  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Do not alter `LZWInputStream` or the factory logic, which already supports [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemory‐limit checks in a reusable manner.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Retain backwards compatibility: callers who explicitly supply a non‐negative [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemory limit continue to work unmodified.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Do not modify or remove API surface; only introduce a default cap when none is[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprovided.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Proposed Patch in `ZCompressorInputStream.java`  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Define a new constant for a safe default memory limit—for example, [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m MiB [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[1;36m1024[0m[39m KiB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[39m** Default max memory for LZW tables: [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m MiB. *[0m[35m/[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      private static final int DEFAULT_MEMORY_LIMIT_KIB = [0m[1;36m1024[0m[39m;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Change the no‐arg constructor to use this default instead of `[0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m`:  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```diff[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       public [0m[1;35mZCompressorInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal InputStream inputStream[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIOException [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m-          [0m[1;35mthis[0m[1;39m([0m[39minputStream, [0m[1;36m-1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+          [0m[1;35mthis[0m[1;39m([0m[39minputStream, DEFAULT_MEMORY_LIMIT_KIB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. In the two‐arg constructor, clamp any negative limit to the default before [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minitializing tables:  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```diff[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       public [0m[1;35mZCompressorInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal InputStream inputStream, final int [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemoryLimitInKiB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException [0m[1;39m{[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m-          [0m[1;35msuper[0m[1;39m([0m[39minputStream, ByteOrder.LITTLE_ENDIAN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+          [0m[1;35msuper[0m[1;39m([0m[39minputStream, ByteOrder.LITTLE_ENDIAN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           final int firstByte = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35min.readBits[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           final int secondByte = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35min.readBits[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           final int thirdByte = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35min.readBits[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[33m...[0m[39m header checks [0m[33m...[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m-          [0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCodeSize, memoryLimitInKiB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Enforce a sane default when caller passes < [0m[1;36m0[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+          final int effectiveLimit = memoryLimitInKiB < [0m[1;36m0[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+                  ? DEFAULT_MEMORY_LIMIT_KIB[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+                  : memoryLimitInKiB;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+          [0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCodeSize, effectiveLimit[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           [0m[1;35mclearEntries[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Security:** By defaulting to a positive cap, any attempt to allocate LZW [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtables beyond [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m MiB will now raise a `MemoryLimitException` instead of causing an [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munbounded allocation and OOM.  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Minimal Impact:** Limits only the `.Z` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLZW[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m decompressor path. Other [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompressor implementations and existing factory logic remain untouched.  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Backward Compatibility:** Users who explicitly pass a `memoryLimitInKiB >= [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m0[0m[39m` or configure a `CompressorStreamFactory` with their own limit will continue to [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhave their limits honored.  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Preserves Functionality:** Typical valid `.Z` streams use a max code size of[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m12[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m bits, requiring at most a few hundred KiB of table state—well under the [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m MiB[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdefault.  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects and Mitigation  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Legitimate Large `.Z` Streams:** In the unlikely event that someone needs to[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdecompress valid `.Z` files with very large code sizes [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., >[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m bits[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, they can [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstill use the two‐arg constructor directly and supply a higher memory limit.  [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Test Coverage:** Add unit tests to confirm that a too‐large `maxCodeSize` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtriggers `MemoryLimitException` rather than OOM. Also verify that typical small [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`.Z` streams decompress normally.  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. References in Codebase  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This pattern mirrors the memory‐limit enforcement in `XZCompressorInputStream`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand `LZMACompressorInputStream`, which accept a `memoryLimitInKiB` parameter and [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39menforce it in their constructors.  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `[0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint maxCodeSize, int memoryLimitKiB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` in [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`LZWInputStream` already contains the logic to throw `MemoryLimitException` when [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39musage exceeds the provided limit. We simply ensure that a non‐negative limit is [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malways passed.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code_range>src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/compressors/z/ZCompressorInpu[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtStream.jav[0m[1;92ma:60[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m90[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
